<P class=ACTION 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt" 
align=center><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">THEY
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">&nbsp;
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">FADE IN:<SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. BEDROOM - 
DAY
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Tiny golden 
wheels and gears turning lazily upon metal rods. Mechanical pieces. Small and 
intricate. Glittering in the sunlight.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">REVEAL
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The gears are 
turning within an ANTIQUE DESK CLOCK sitting on a book shelf, a small pendulum 
swinging back and forth behind the glass housing.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The room is 
barren except for a pair of open suitcases and a bed that's been stripped. 
Sitting on the mattress is ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA LEVIN 
...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Smart and 
clever. Dressed in a graduation gown and staring out the window. She seems to be 
lost in thought, immobile, until the bedroom door swings open and ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">CONNOR LEVIN, 
aged seventeen and wearing a suit and tie, steps inside.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">CONNOR
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Dad says we 
gotta get moving. We're late.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">I'm getting 
ready.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">CONNOR
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">You're sitting 
on the bed.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=PARENTHETICAL 
style="TEXT-INDENT: -7pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">(dryly)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Thanks for 
clearing that up. I'll be right down.<SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">He steps 
out.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia takes a 
framed picture out of her suitcase -- a candid shot of herself standing with her 
MOTHER, forties, a healthy and vibrant woman.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA<SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: none"> (cont'd)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Sure do miss 
you.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Above her, a 
CEILING FAN rotates. Creating a soft HUMMING.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">EXT. WESTWOOD - 
APARTMENT BUILDING - DAY
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia walks out 
of the building where her father, GUY LEVIN, an older man with a kind face, 
waits. Connor is checking his reflection in the car window, adjusting his tie, 
fussing with his hair.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">GUY
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">You ready?
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">All set. I 
packed up everything.
<P class=PARENTHETICAL 
style="TEXT-INDENT: -7pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">(remembering)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Oh, except 
Mom's clock -- I think there's something wrong with it. It's not telling the 
right time.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">GUY
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">I'll get it 
fixed. Probably just needs a few new parts.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Guy smiles at 
Julia for a moment. Very warmly.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">GUY<SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: none"> (cont'd)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">You look just 
like your mother.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia is 
momentarily uncomfortable. But she recovers, smiles and kisses her father on the 
cheek.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">We'll be 
late.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">EXT. UNIVERSITY 
OF CALIFORNIA, LOS ANGELES - CAMPUS - DAY
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Students 
dressed in graduation caps and gowns are gathered on the campus grounds.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia stands by 
herself, taking pictures with a professional Nikon camera. She focuses the 
camera upon ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">TERRY ALBA, 22, 
beautiful and sexy. Very particular and demanding. She smiles perfectly as Julia 
snaps the picture. But her boyfriend, SAM BURNSIDE, cute and mischievous, 
sporting pink hair and loud clothes, makes a face.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Winding her 
film, Julia searches a moment, then smiles. Raising her camera lens, she snaps a 
picture of ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">PAUL LOOMIS 
...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Early twenties. 
Dark hair. Strapping and perfectly handsome. He wears a blue and gold striped 
tie with his starched white shirt and graduation gown.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">He kisses her. 
Passionate and gentle.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">PAUL
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">You packed 
up?
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Ready to move 
in. I'll be storing some of the stuff you've already got. Television. CD player. 
Microwave.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">PAUL
<P class=PARENTHETICAL 
style="TEXT-INDENT: -7pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">(suggestively)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Bed.<SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia smiles at 
him.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Bed.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">PAUL
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Med School 
doesn't start until August. At least not for the freshmen, so we've got plenty 
of time to see Europe, take the car trip up north ...
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">I hope it won't 
be a drag. There's a lot of stuff to move out of my mother's cabin.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">PAUL
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Our friends 
will be there. It'll be fun.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">I hope so.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Beat.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">PAUL
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">You okay?
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Tense.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">PAUL
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Would it help 
if I massaged your breasts?
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">No.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">PAUL
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Because it 
would help me.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=PARENTHETICAL 
style="TEXT-INDENT: -7pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">(stifling 
laughter)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Maybe 
later.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The students 
start forming into lines.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA<SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: none"> (cont'd)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Hey, I saw your 
Mom and kid sister. Where's your Dad?
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Beat.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">PAUL
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">He's not 
coming.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">But it's your 
graduation.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul shrugs 
again. A brief sting of hurt on his face.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME

<P class=CHARACTERNAME

<P class=ACTION

<P class=ACTION

<P class=ACTION

<P class=SCENEHEADING

<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul and Terry

<P class=ACTION

<P class=ACTION

<P class=ACTION

<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">SAM ...
<P class=ACTION

<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">THE DRAWING IS

<P class=ACTION

<P class=ACTION

<P class=ACTION

<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia looks

<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">More HISSING. 
Unmistakable this time. A diminutive SCRAPING, almost like fingernails raking on

<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She moves 
towards the sound.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. CABIN - 
HALLWAY - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia creeps

are closed shut.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The SCRAPING 
sound rises up again. Much closer. Behind one of the bedroom doors. 
Beckoning.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia reaches 
out for the doorknob.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. CABIN - 
BEDROOM - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The door opens. 
Julia's stomach rises into her throat. Terror floods her face.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">Resting on the bed is a BODY BAG. So smeared 
with blood that the corpse inside isn't visible except for its massive 
bulk.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">Something SCRATCHES on the BODY BAG from 
INSIDE.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia's body 
goes rigid. She can't force herself to move.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">The body bag is slowly unzipped from the 
inside. Stretching down the length of the plastic until the bag is wide open. 
The corpse inside is still hidden. 
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">As if drawn by 
some alien force, Julia moves to the bed. Her entire body is shaking.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She reaches out 
and carefully peels back the plastic.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Resting within 
the body bag is THE LITTLE GIRL. Eyes puffed shut. Hair slicked with blood. Her 
skin is livid. Her face is ghostly white and smeared with crimson gore.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia is frozen 
in place. Heart pounding. Terrified.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">THE GIRL'S EYES 
BLINK OPEN AS SHE SHRIEKS BLOODY MURDER.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. CABIN - 
LIVING ROOM - MORNING
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia is 
startled awake and groggily looks around the room. Paul and Terry are still in

<P class=ACTION

<P class=PARENTHETICAL

<P class=ACTION

<P class=ACTION

<P class=ACTION

style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">There are several pieces of metal littering

style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul reaches

enclosed by pine trees. A few birds are singing overhead.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul enters the 
forest, pushing back branches, following the trail of discarded metal until he 
freezes ... his eyes staring directly ahead at ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">CLUMPS OF BLACK 
SKIN ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Hanging from 
branches. Scattered on the ground. Like the skin of a snake which has been 
shed.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul is 
completely unsettled. He kneels down, picking up a flap of skin from the ground, 
peeling it away from a steel ROD dripping with oozing slime. Holds it up. It's 
still black in color but almost transparent in the murky light.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The wind HISSES 
through the trees, mussing Paul's hair.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul drops the 
piece of skin on the ground.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The birds 
abruptly stop singing in unison. The WIND CEASES.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul looks 
around the forest. The sudden quiet has got him spooked. His arms and legs 
stiffen. Paul can't even bring himself to move or breathe ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">UNTIL SOMETHING 
DROPS ON HIS SHOULDER ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul freaks and 
whirls around, grabbing his shoulder to find
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">A PIECE OF SKIN 
...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Clinging to 
him. He rips it off and sprints for the footpath.
<P class=SCENEHEADING

FOOTPATH - DAY
<P class=ACTION

<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Behind him, the 
wind HISSES through the trees again.

four of us. You. Me. Paul. Sam.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry is 
shaking now. Complete fright.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">TERRY
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">They got to 
you. They got to you.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Nobody got to 
me.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry starts 
collecting her things.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">TERRY
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Look, could you 
drop me off at my brother's apartment? I need to pick up some things before I go 
to the airport.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Where are you 
going?
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">TERRY
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">To see my 
parents.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">You can't just 
leave.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry starts 
weeping. Grabbing her legs and squeezing them.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">TERRY
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">They put things 
in my legs so they can track me. It hurts.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=PARENTHETICAL 
style="TEXT-INDENT: -7pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">(very 
concerned)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry? What can 
I do to help you?
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry takes her 
hand. Her eyes pleading.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">TERRY
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Remember me. 
Please remember me.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">From the street 
outside the car, the sound of a TODDLER CRYING can be heard. Terry's head snaps 
around. She stares out the windshield at the screaming child.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">TERRY<SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: none"> (cont'd)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">They found me 
again.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Before Julia 
can react, Terry bolts from the car.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry!
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia 
pursues.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">EXT. SAN 
FRANCISCO - STREET - LATE AFTERNOON
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia pushes 
and shoves her way along the sidewalk. Terry is running like a madwoman. Pure 
unabated terror.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry rushes 
down into a subway entrance. Julia follows.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. SUBWAY 
STATION - LATE AFTERNOON
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">People are 
crowded on the platform, waiting as a BART train rushes into the station.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The doors open. 
Passengers move off the train. Others get on.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia rushes 
down the stairs and pushes past the arriving commuters. There's no sign of 
Terry. Julia keeps searching. Looks right. Then left. Finally, she spots Terry 
boarding the BART train.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry! 
Wait!
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia rushes 
forward, squirming through the crowd, until she reaches the doors just as they 
SLAM CLOSED. She looks through the windows, trying to find Terry amongst the 
crowd inside.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The train 
starts to move.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Standing at one 
of the train's passenger windows, his face and palms pressed against the glass, 
is --
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">THE BLOND BOY 
IN THE SUPERMAN SHIRT.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Staring 
directly at her. Dark circles around his eyes.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">He smiles at 
Julia.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">His teeth are made of metal.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia stands 
thunderstruck. The BOY in the window moves past.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The train 
shoots into the awaiting tunnel. Julia is left standing frozen and immobile on 
the platform.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Near the subway 
entrance, a HOMELESS MAN with HOOKS FOR HANDS is convulsing as he sits against 
the wall. Eyes wide open. Shaking horribly and staring at nothing.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. APARTMENT 
BUILDING - UPSTAIRS HALLWAY - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Quiet and dimly 
lit. Several of the lights are burnt out, leaving the hallway drowning in 
shadows.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The elevator 
doors open. Terry exits and moves quickly down the hallway. Her face is 
terrified. Sick.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She arrives at 
an apartment. Terry fumbles with her keys.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">A soft<SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase"> THUMPING in the hallway. Deep and 
hollow. Terry spins around, the keys JINGLING in her hand.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Nothing there. 
The hall appears to be empty and dark. One of the lights overhead is flickering 
and buzzing softly, providing 
scant illumination.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She takes a 
step back ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">A soft TINKLING 
sound at her feet. Terry looks down to find a few pieces of METAL littering the 
floor. Nuts and bolts. Rods. Alien in design.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry's 
paranoia rises to a fever pitch. She turns the key in the lock. Opens the front 
door.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. APARTMENT 
- LIVING ROOM - NIGHT
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: none">Terry shuts the door. Locks it. Switches on the 
lights. Drops her KEYS and CELL PHONE on a coffee table.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: none">She moves briskly into --
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. APARTMENT 
- BEDROOM - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">An open 
suitcase on the bed. Terry snatches up a PLANE TICKET and jams the ticket folder 
into her purse. Slams the suitcase closed.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. APARTMENT 
- LIVING ROOM - CONTINUOUS
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry leaves 
the bedroom, carrying the suitcase, and walks straight towards the front door. 
She collects her keys and her cell phone from the table.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">The lights in the apartment simultaneously go 
out.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry is caught 
entirely off guard. She spins around to face the living room. Nobody's there. 
Nothing.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">SOMETHING BANGS 
AT THE FRONT DOOR. A STEADY POUNDING. THE BANGING GOES ON FOR A FEW SECONDS AND 
THEN STOPS DEAD.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry's 
breathing quickens. She puts the suitcase down.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">A crack of 
THUNDER reverberates outside.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Moving with the 
cautious steps of a small child, she walks towards the front door. Foot by foot. 
The only sound is her FRIGHTENED BREATHING. She arrives at the peephole and 
looks out into the empty hall.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">SOMETHING 
STARES BACK AT HER THROUGH THE PEEPHOLE.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Moving right in 
front of the door. One of its yellow eyes piercing through ... surrounded by 
midnight skin pierced with metal bolts and rods.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">TERRY SCREAMS 
HER LUNGS OUT.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The DOOR 
RATTLES like it's going to break off its hinges. Something SLAMS REPEATEDLY 
against the wood.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry tears 
through the apartment, feet POUNDING. She rushes into the bedroom.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The front door 
in the living room BREAKS OPEN.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. APARTMENT 
- BEDROOM - CONTINUOUS
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry SLAMS the 
bedroom door and locks it. Backs away towards the bed, when ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">A HAND REACHES 
OUT FROM UNDER IT ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Grabbing hold 
of her ankle. Fused together from rotting flesh, human parts, and metal pieces. 
Terry pitches forward, SCREAMING, falling to her hands and knees.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The hand starts 
dragging her under the bed.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry kicks and 
claws on the floor. Somehow manages to free herself from the hand's grip. She 
goes for the window and pulls it open. Steps outside.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The entire bed 
is OVERTURNED and tossed aside.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">EXT. APARTMENT 
BUILDING - FIRE ESCAPE - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry is 
immediately drenched by the storm. The door within her bedroom can be heard 
CRASHING OPEN, followed by a ROARING unlike anything on this earth.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry rushes 
down the fire escape, FEET BANGING on the metal steps. But she stops dead in her 
tracks when she notices --
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">SEVERAL FIGURES 
...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Standing in the 
alley far below. Looking up at her. Waiting.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">A sound rises 
up behind her. THE SOUND OF FOOTSTEPS BANGING DOWN THE FIRE ESCAPE IN 
PURSUIT.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">TERRY
<P class=PARENTHETICAL 
style="TEXT-INDENT: -7pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">(horrified)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Oh God ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry 
desperately goes to a window. She pulls it open, stepping inside, THE BANGING 
FOOTSTEPS RIGHT BEHIND HER. 
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. APARTMENT 
BUILDING - HALLWAY - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The apartment 
floor is being renovated. Plastic tarps cover the doors and windows. Terry races 
through the hallway, SCREAMING WILDLY as she POUNDS on the doors.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">TERRY
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">HELP ME! PLEASE 
HELP!!!
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry rockets 
around the corner. She presses the elevator door button frantically.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The sound of 
CROAKING and HISSING fills the hallway.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The elevator 
doors slide open.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry lunges 
into the elevator, hits for the lobby, then starts BEATING FRENZIEDLY on the 
door close button.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Several shadows 
appear in the hallway. Getting closer.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry SCREAMS 
WILDLY and keeps pounding the button.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The bizarre 
HISSING becomes a FRIGHTFUL ROAR just as ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The elevator 
doors pull shut. Closing on the unseen things in the hallway.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. ELEVATOR - 
NIGHT
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: none">The car starts going down. Floor lights blink above 
the door.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: none">8 ... 7 ... 6 ...
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: none">Terry punches out 9-1-1 on the<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; cell phone's keypad. Nothing comes 
through the receiver. Only static.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">TERRY
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Come on ... 
come on ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She dials 
again.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">4 ... 3 ... 2 
...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">More static 
over the cell phone. Terry has started crying in anguish when the elevator comes 
to an abrupt halt.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The doors stay 
closed.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry looks 
above the elevator doors. The floor light reads --
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">"B" 
(Basement)
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry starts 
pressing for the lobby. The elevator won't move. She presses the "door open" 
button, the alarm button, anything at all. Nothing responds.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">TERRY<SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: none"> (cont'd)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">HELP! SOMEBODY! 
HELP ME!!!
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Nothing. Futile 
silence. She's about to try dialing on the cell phone again, when ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">WHUMP. A heavy 
thudding sound above the elevator car roof. The light overhead flickers like a 
candle. Terry gazes at the failing light, then tracks her eyes towards the trap 
door in the roof.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">A few more hollow THUMPS.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry is 
petrified. She takes a step backward. The light flashes off and on again ... 
creating a strobe light effect.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Behind her, the 
elevator doors silently pull open.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Terry's gaze is 
still focussed on the ceiling trap door. Behind her, the basement is pitch 
black. She continues moving backwards towards the open elevator doors, step 
after step, completely unaware ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">UNTIL SOMETHING 
LEAPS OUT OF THE DARK AND GRABS HER.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">In the moment 
it takes to draw a breath and scream, it's already over.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The light goes 
out.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. APARTMENT 
BUILDING - UPSTAIRS HALLWAY - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The lobby is 
vacant and terribly still. The elevator doors remain closed, a few THUMPING 
sounds coming from the shaft far below.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Then 
nothing.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">EXT. SAN 
FRANCISCO - STREET - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The sound of a 
PHONE LINE RINGING.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia is 
sitting inside of the parked Range Rover, the cell phone pressed against her 
ear.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">MAN'S VOICE
<P class=PARENTHETICAL 
style="TEXT-INDENT: -7pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">(from 
phone)
<P class=DIALOG

knife into the sink and pinches the wound. Squeezing hard.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">A speck of metal flashes inSIDE the 
wound.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia continues 
squeezing, tears rolling, fingernails digging into the wound as ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">THE TIP OF A 
METAL SPLINTER PUSHES UP THROUGH THE BLOOD. 
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia starts 
pulling it out of her finger. The splinter rises from the wound ... and rises 
... and rises ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">More blood 
spatters into the sink.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia is 
GASPING and CRYING as the pain becomes excruciating. The glittering splinter is 
five inches long and growing.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">The splinter is pulled out. It's seven inches 
long.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia drops the 
splinter into the sink. She moves away from the counter, back towards the living 
room, unbelieving, horrified ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She stumbles 
towards the door.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. COFFEE 
SHOP - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia walks out 
of the restroom. Stops cold.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Everyone in the 
coffee shop is staring at her. The customers. The waiters.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The lights are 
dimming. A lack of power.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia forces 
herself to move. She goes to her table, picks up the photographs, and suddenly 
notices that in the graduation pictures --
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">SAM AND TERRY 
HAVE DISAPPEARED. ALMOST AS IF THEY NEVER WERE A PART OF THE PHOTOS. PAUL AND 
JULIA ARE TOGETHER IN EVERY PICTURE -- ALONE.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia grabs the 
photographs and turns around.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The customers 
in the coffee shop are standing now. Their eyes are dark shadows. Something 
about the way they stand is completely unnatural. All wrong.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Panic begins to 
settle in. Julia quickly walks to the door.

<P class=CHARACTERNAME

<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia races 
across the intersection and streaks towards the subway station entrance.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">EXT. SUBWAY 
STATION ENTRANCE - STAIRS - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul is nowhere 
to be found. The stairs are empty.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul?!
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia looks 
around desperately. She can't find him in the crowds on the sidewalks. She turns 
and looks down the stairs towards the open entryway to the subway system.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul is walking 
through the entryway. A friend with him is patting him on the shoulder. Just 
after Paul has disappeared through the entryway, the friend turns around.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">IT'S SAM.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">His lips are 
parched, pitch black eyes bulging, his features somehow more twisted and 
unfamiliar. His face twitches as he stares coldly at Julia, and he runs.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt"><SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: uppercase">Small pieces of metal drop from Sam's pants 
legs as he disappears through the entryway.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA 
(cont'd)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">PAUL!
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She frantically 
rushes down the stairs.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA<SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: none"> (cont'd)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">THAT'S NOT 
SAM!!! PAUL!!!
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She rushes 
through the entryway.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. SUBWAY 
STATION - UPPER LEVEL - CONTINUOUS
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The upper level 
is almost completely empty save a few kids and late-night commuters. Julia is 
hysterical now. The first time we've seen her lose control.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She looks 
around frantically. Spots Paul and Sam going down the escalator together.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul!
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia rushes 
towards the turnstiles. Jumps them. A GUARD steps out of his booth.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">GUARD
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Hey! You need a 
ticket! Hey!!!
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She keeps 
going.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. SUBWAY 
STATION - PLATFORM - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul and Sam 
reach the bottom of the escalators. They move towards the platform. The lights 
start twinkling. Losing power.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">PAUL
<P class=PARENTHETICAL 
style="TEXT-INDENT: -7pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">(confused)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">I thought you 
said she'd be here.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Sam smirks 
back, mute ... and GRABS HIM BY THE THROAT.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The lights GO 
OUT.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. SUBWAY 
STATION - ESCALATOR - CONTINUOUS
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia bolts 
down the escalator.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. SUBWAY 
STATION - PLATFORM - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She reaches the 
platform and rushes to the center.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">There's nobody 
else down there. The lights are flickering. Slowly, they return to normal.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=PARENTHETICAL 
style="TEXT-INDENT: -7pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">(calling)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul?!
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">No 
response.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">A train RUMBLES 
through the station. Julia moves to the opposite side and looks.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Resting on the 
tracks, leading into the tunnel, are a trail of metal pieces. Exactly like the 
ones from the cabin.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia looks 
back. The GUARD is coming down the escalator.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Without 
hesitation, she jumps down to the tracks. Moving quickly and bending down to 
avoid being seen, she rushes into the awaiting subway tunnel.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. SUBWAY 
TUNNEL - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Drowned in 
shadows. An unnatural silence fills the tunnel.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia moves 
cautiously amongst the tracks. Eyes scanning the darkness. Following the trail 
of discarded metal.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">A SHARP 
HISSING.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia spins 
around. A few more HISSING SOUNDS rise from electrical sparks on the tracks. 
Blue light flashes within the tunnel. Then, it ceases.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She turns back 
to continue her search, wind sifting through her hair, when she finds --
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">A LARGE 
HOLE
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">At the base of 
the subway wall. Julia reaches down and palms a few metal pieces at the base of 
the hole.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She peers 
inside. A dull flickering light flashes within.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia takes a 
calming breath. She moves into the hole.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. CRAWL 
SPACE - CONTINUOUS
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">A narrow and 
claustrophobic space. Julia squirms through the confined space, pulling herself 
towards the flashing light.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. CORRIDOR - 
CONTINUOUS
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia pulls 
herself through another opening and finds herself standing in the threshold of a 
corridor. Both the walls and floor are constructed of crude metal grates and 
long pipes. Anything could be hiding within. Waiting.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She moves 
slowly into the corridor, a STROBE LIGHT flickering around her. She gropes 
towards another opening.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The sound of 
her TERRIFIED BREATHING is slowly replaced by the RHYTHMIC HUMMING OF 
MACHINES.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. STAIRWELL 
- CONTINUOUS
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Steam rises 
from the pipes. Bathing the stairwell in mist.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The fluorescent 
lights above are glimmering in the darkness. Julia stands at the top of the 
stairwell. She can't even see the bottom of the steps.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Carefully, she 
starts moving down. Her hand gripping the metal railing.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The HUMMING OF 
MACHINES grows louder ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Her foot 
accidentally kicks a few pieces of metal on the steps. A light CLINKING as the 
metal scatters down ahead of her.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The HUMMING OF 
MACHINES is closer now. Just beyond the sheathing clouds of blue and white 
mist.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The metal 
railing is suddenly replaced by HUMAN BONES.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia pulls her 
hand away from the railing. Looks skyward and discovers more BONES are being 
used to brace the ceiling along with metal beams.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She stops. 
Shutting her eyes in fear. Starts to lose control.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">From somewhere 
within, she manages to steady herself. Keeps going through the awaiting steam 
curtain at the bottom.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. MAIN 
HALLWAYS - CONTINUOUS
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The steam parts 
to reveal a dark space. Cold and damp.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia moves 
into the main hallway, stumbling through a hallway that can best be described as 
a living nightmare. Mammoth pipes and human skin has been fashioned together 
into a wall, pulsating with the HEARTBEAT OF MACHINES that saturates the entire 
hallway.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Steam jets into 
the hallway intermittently from the pipes. Creating great clouds.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia is beyond 
horrified. Her face registers a numbness. Complete and total astonishment.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Human bones and 
body parts have been so expertly fashioned into the corridor that it's 
impossible to distinguish where the organic ends and the mechanical begins.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She enters 
another corridor. Her face is struck by a JET OF HISSING STEAM.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She presses 
onward. Slipping past the skulls and littered metal on the floor.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Another BLAST 
OF STEAM.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Something leaps 
out of the middle of it.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia whirls 
back around a corner, pressing flat against the wall as a BLACK SHAPE moves 
through the steam. Unidentifiable features. Movements that suggest nothing by 
chaos and madness.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The SHAPE 
HISSES and CROAKS in the hallway.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia waits. 
She doesn't even breathe. The HISSING stops.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She gradually 
turns to peek back into the hallway where the thing once stood.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">CLOSE ON 
JULIA'S EYES
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">as she looks 
around the corner. The shape has disappeared.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Carefully she 
keeps going forward. Drenched in water and sweat. Slipping through the steam 
clouds that mask another entrance.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. LAIR - 
NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">A massive room 
where empty human skins are dangling from hooks, complete and preserved from 
head to toe. The skins sway and rock gently in the draft. Thousands of them.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia moves 
towards the center of the room.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">A large 
OPERATING TABLE awaits. But the surface of the table is sunken like a water 
basin. Next to the table is a pedestal littered with BLOODY INSTRUMENTS. Cutting 
tools. Knives. Curved hooks.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia notices 
that Paul's torn clothes are resting at the foot of the table. Shirt shredded to 
a rag. Sneakers orphaned nearby. Jeans spattered with blood.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Her breathing 
quickens. Her heart POUNDING.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She reaches the 
foot of the table. Paul is lying within the basin, completely naked and 
partially covered with LITTERED BODY PARTS. Organs and entrails. 
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The basin is 
filled with water and blood. An immobile form is resting next to him.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia moves 
quickly. She tries to wake him up.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul. Paul, 
wake up.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">He stirs. His 
nose crinkles slightly.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA<SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: none"> (cont'd)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Wake up.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She grabs him 
and lifts him up. He starts COUGHING.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA<SPAN 
style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: none"> (cont'd)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">You've gotta 
hurry.
<P class=PARENTHETICAL 
style="TEXT-INDENT: -7pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">(then)
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Here ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia grabs his 
jeans. She helps him slide down from the basin and he pulls them on.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">A skinned HAND 
grabs hers. Julia yelps a SCREAM.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The other form 
-- a thing in the basin -- rises 
and turns. Slicked with blood. Empty sockets where the eyes should be. Mouth 
falling open. A horror that shouldn't be alive.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia SCREAMS 
again.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Her free hand 
grabs a HOOK from the pedestal and swings the blade into the thing's neck. Blood 
fountains up.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The thing 
begins SHRIEKING.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">With Paul 
leaning on her for support, Julia rapidly heads for the door.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. MAIN 
HALLWAYS - CONTINUOUS
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia navigates 
her way through the hallways. Moving blindly through sudden JETS OF STEAM, the 
sound of MACHINES around them. Paul leans on her, his eyes remaining closed, 
COUGHING and stumbling.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA'S POV
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Racing through 
the halls. The steam clouds suddenly EXPLODING into her view. 
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. STAIRWELL 
- CONTINUOUS
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia reaches 
the stairwell and helps Paul climb the steps. She looks back over her shoulder. 
Nothing behind them.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. CORRIDOR - 
CONTINUOUS
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia stops at 
the corridor opening. The strobe light FLASHES within. Clicking.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The corridor 
looks empty. Nothing but pipes and shadows.
<P class=CHARACTERNAME 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA
<P class=DIALOG 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">We're almost 
there.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia turns to 
Paul and finds a face with glaring yellow eyes and metal teeth. He stares back 
at her.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">A moment of 
sheer horror. Julia reels back into the corridor. Pressed flat against the wall. 
Sliding towards the crawl space opening.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul starts 
advancing into the corridor. Grinning with teeth that flash with every click of 
the strobe light.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She keeps 
sliding away ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">He grabs his 
chest and RIPS IT OPEN, tearing the covering skin apart as he would a shirt. A 
menagerie of human bones and metal are revealed behind it.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia tries to 
scream. Eyes wide. She can't make a sound.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Paul tears the 
skin covering his chest wider. Pulling it away. Stripping himself clean.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia reaches 
the crawl space. Sliding down.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The last pieces 
Paul's skin are torn off. The thing that had been pretending to be Paul stands 
in his place.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Only brief 
glimpses are allowed by the strobe light. An abysm of immemorial lunacy 
consisting of fashioned human parts and twisted metal. A human heart beating 
within exposed ribs. Bones combined with pulleys and rods. The face of a skull. 
A contradiction of all matter and cosmic order.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia slips 
back into the crawl space. Still trying to scream.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. CRAWL 
SPACE - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia drags 
herself through the crawl space. Moving quickly. Panicked.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. SUBWAY 
TUNNEL - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia squeezes 
herself through the exposed hole. She kicks to her feet and tears off into the 
tunnel.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. SUBWAY 
TUNNEL - STATION OPENING - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia has 
almost reached the platform opening for the train.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">BEHIND HER, A 
CHORUS OF PURSUING MONSTROUS SCREAMS RISE UP WITHIN THE TUNNEL.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. SUBWAY 
STATION - PLATFORM - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia runs 
directly parallel to the subway platform. The lights alongside of her start 
flickering and go out, one by one, as she advances.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">THE HISSING AND 
SCREAMING CONTINUES TO RISE.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She reaches the 
opposite tunnel and grabs hold of the platform, pulling herself up. The platform 
goes dark.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Appearing out 
of the far tunnel are a DOZEN DARK SHAPES, scampering along the walls and 
running on all fours across the tracks. Their characteristics barely 
visible.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia kicks 
back as the shrieking things bear down on her, yellow eyes flaring in the dark, 
metal teeth flashing.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia tries to 
run for the escalator, but the things cover the walls behind the tracks. Ready 
to spring.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Finally, one of 
the monsters does leap towards her ...
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">AND IS SMASHED 
TO BITS BY AN APPROACHING BART TRAIN.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Reducing the 
monster to a few vestiges of scattered metal. The other creatures on the tracks 
are also run down.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia watches 
as the train RUMBLES past. And then, silence.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Nothing is left 
except for a few swirling newspapers. The lights flicker and come back to 
life.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Rising up to 
her feet, rescued from death by chance, Julia starts backing towards the 
escalator. Her eyes locked upon the darkened tunnel before she turns and races 
up.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">EXT. SUBWAY 
STATION ENTRANCE - STAIRS - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Rain has 
started falling again. Pelting the stairs.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia dashes up 
the stairwell and sprints into the street. She doesn't look back.
<P class=TRANSITION 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt" 
align=right>DISSOLVE TO:
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">EXT. SAN 
FRANCISCO - STREET - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">The rain falls 
so heavily that it creates a dense, blue FOG which shrouds the entire 
street.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia appears 
through the storm, running towards a telephone booth on the street corner. She 
rips open the door, steps inside, and slams the door shut.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. PHONE 
BOOTH - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">She drops a few 
quarters into the phone. Dials. And waits.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. LEVIN 
HOUSE - LIVING ROOM - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Dark and still. 
Lightning frames the windows. The picture of Julia and her mother rests near a 
phone as the line RINGS.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Guy comes 
downstairs and answers the portable.

<P class=ACTION

<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. PHONE 
BOOTH - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION

is abruptly cut off.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Julia begins to 
cry. She covers her face with her hands. The tears roll through her fingers.
<P class=SCENEHEADING 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">INT. LEVIN 
RESIDENCE - LIVING ROOM - NIGHT
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Guy stares at 
the phone for a moment.&nbsp; A strange 
feeling. Something isn't right. He thinks a moment. Then shakes it off and heads 
upstairs, moving directly past the picture next to the phone.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">JULIA IS GONE. 
VANISHED FROM THE PICTURE WITHOUT A TRACE. ONLY HER MOTHER REMAINS.
<P class=ACTION 
style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-line-height-alt: 9.0pt">Lightning 
flashes across the picture's glass frame.
